
============== high level task decomposition ================
[{'objective': 'Calculate the volume of tetrahedron ABCD using the given edge lengths.'}, {'objective': 'Compute the total surface area of tetrahedron ABCD by finding the areas of all four triangular faces.'}, {'objective': 'Determine the inradius (equal distance from the interior point to each face) using the formula inradius = 3 * volume / surface area.'}, {'objective': 'Express the inradius in the form (m√n)/p with m, n, p positive integers, m and p coprime, n square-free, and find m + n + p.'}]
============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- The problem involves a tetrahedron named ABCD.
- The lengths of edges are given as follows:
  * AB = CD = √41
  * AC = BD = √80
  * BC = AD = √89
- There exists a point I inside the tetrahedron such that the perpendicular distances from I to each of the four faces of the tetrahedron are equal.
- The equal distance from point I to each face can be expressed in the form \( \frac{m \sqrt{n}}{p} \), where m, n, p are positive integers, m and p are coprime, and n is square-free.

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- The tetrahedron ABCD has pairs of edges equal in length, indicating some symmetry or special geometric property.
- The equalities AB=CD, AC=BD, and BC=AD suggest that opposite edges have equal lengths, which is a notable constraint affecting the shape.
- The point I inside the tetrahedron with equal distances to all faces implies that I is the incenter of the tetrahedron (the center of the inscribed sphere).
- The condition of equal distances to faces (equal face-to-point perpendicular distances) is a strong geometric constraint that relates the position of I to the tetrahedron’s dimensions.
- The problem’s structure suggests that the tetrahedron is not arbitrary but has a special configuration allowing an inscribed sphere with a well-defined inradius.

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem lies primarily in the domain of solid geometry (3D Euclidean geometry).
- It involves concepts of tetrahedra, edge lengths, face distances, and centers related to inscribed spheres.
- Subfields include metric geometry and spatial reasoning.
- Such problems commonly appear in mathematical competitions and advanced geometry contexts.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- The problem does not explicitly state whether the tetrahedron is convex, but the existence of an interior point I with equal distances to faces implies convexity.
- The exact coordinates or angles of the tetrahedron are not given, so the shape must be inferred from edge lengths and symmetry.
- The problem assumes the existence of the incenter but does not provide explicit construction or verification.
- Potential challenges include verifying the tetrahedron’s realizability with the given edge lengths and computing the inradius without explicit coordinates.
- The notation and conditions on m, n, p imply simplification and rationalization steps that may be nontrivial.

async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_sc_instruction_0 = "Sub-task 1: Aggregate and combine the given edge lengths to verify the tetrahedron's properties and prepare for volume and area calculations. Given the edge lengths AB=CD=sqrt(41), AC=BD=sqrt(80), BC=AD=sqrt(89), analyze the tetrahedron's symmetry and verify the consistency of these lengths."
    N0 = self.max_sc
    cot_sc_agents_0 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N0)]
    possible_answers_0 = []
    possible_thinkings_0 = []
    subtask_desc_0 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_0,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N0):
        thinking0, answer0 = await cot_sc_agents_0[i]([taskInfo], cot_sc_instruction_0, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_sc_agents_0[i].id}, verifying tetrahedron properties, thinking: {thinking0.content}; answer: {answer0.content}")
        possible_answers_0.append(answer0)
        possible_thinkings_0.append(thinking0)
    final_decision_agent_0 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking0, answer0 = await final_decision_agent_0([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_0 + possible_answers_0, "Sub-task 1: Synthesize and confirm tetrahedron properties and edge length consistency.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking0.content}; answer - {answer0.content}")
    subtask_desc_0['response'] = {"thinking": thinking0, "answer": answer0}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_0)
    print("Step 0: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    reflexion_instruction_1a = "Sub-task 1: Derive the face areas of the tetrahedron using the given edge lengths and symmetry properties. Use the edge lengths and any symmetry to find the areas of faces ABC, ABD, ACD, and BCD."
    reflexion_instruction_1b = "Sub-task 2: Compute the volume of the tetrahedron using the edge lengths and derived face areas or by applying a suitable formula such as the Cayley-Menger determinant."
    cot_agent_1a = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    cot_agent_1b = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_1a = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_1b = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)

    cot_inputs_1a = [taskInfo, thinking0, answer0]
    thinking1a, answer1a = await cot_agent_1a(cot_inputs_1a, reflexion_instruction_1a, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_1a.id}, deriving face areas, thinking: {thinking1a.content}; answer: {answer1a.content}")

    for i in range(self.max_round):
        feedback1a, correct1a = await critic_agent_1a([taskInfo, thinking1a, answer1a], "Please review the answer above and criticize on where might be wrong. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_1a.id}, feedback on face areas, thinking: {feedback1a.content}; answer: {correct1a.content}")
        if correct1a.content.strip() == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_1a.extend([thinking1a, answer1a, feedback1a])
        thinking1a, answer1a = await cot_agent_1a(cot_inputs_1a, reflexion_instruction_1a, i+1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_1a.id}, refining face areas, thinking: {thinking1a.content}; answer: {answer1a.content}")

    cot_inputs_1b = [taskInfo, thinking0, answer0, thinking1a, answer1a]
    thinking1b, answer1b = await cot_agent_1b(cot_inputs_1b, reflexion_instruction_1b, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_1b.id}, computing volume, thinking: {thinking1b.content}; answer: {answer1b.content}")

    for i in range(self.max_round):
        feedback1b, correct1b = await critic_agent_1b([taskInfo, thinking1b, answer1b], "Please review the answer above and criticize on where might be wrong. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_1b.id}, feedback on volume, thinking: {feedback1b.content}; answer: {correct1b.content}")
        if correct1b.content.strip() == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_1b.extend([thinking1b, answer1b, feedback1b])
        thinking1b, answer1b = await cot_agent_1b(cot_inputs_1b, reflexion_instruction_1b, i+1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_1b.id}, refining volume, thinking: {thinking1b.content}; answer: {answer1b.content}")

    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking1a.content} | {thinking1b.content}; answer - {answer1a.content} | {answer1b.content}")
    subtask_desc_1 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1_and_2",
        "instruction": "Derive face areas and volume with Reflexion",
        "context": ["user query", thinking0.content, answer0.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion",
        "response": {"thinking": [thinking1a, thinking1b], "answer": [answer1a, answer1b]}
    }
    logs.append(subtask_desc_1)
    print("Step 1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_2 = "Sub-task 1: Derive and validate the formula for the inradius (distance from incenter to each face) using the volume and total surface area of the tetrahedron. Use the volume and face areas from previous subtasks to express the inradius."
    N2 = self.max_sc
    cot_sc_agents_2 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N2)]
    possible_answers_2 = []
    possible_thinkings_2 = []
    subtask_desc_2 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_2,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1a.content, answer1a.content, thinking1b.content, answer1b.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N2):
        thinking2, answer2 = await cot_sc_agents_2[i]([taskInfo, thinking1a, answer1a, thinking1b, answer1b], cot_sc_instruction_2, is_sub_task=True)

        possible_answers_2.append(answer2)
        possible_thinkings_2.append(thinking2)
    final_decision_agent_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking2, answer2 = await final_decision_agent_2([taskInfo, thinking1a, answer1a, thinking1b, answer1b] + possible_thinkings_2 + possible_answers_2, "Sub-task 1: Synthesize and validate inradius formula.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3 output: thinking - {thinking2.content}; answer - {answer2.content}")
    subtask_desc_2['response'] = {"thinking": thinking2, "answer": answer2}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_2)
    print("Step 2: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_3 = "Sub-task 1: Compute the inradius explicitly by substituting the volume and surface area values, simplifying the expression to the form (m√n)/p with m, n, p positive integers, m and p coprime, and n square-free."
    N3 = self.max_sc
    cot_sc_agents_3 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N3)]
    possible_answers_3 = []
    possible_thinkings_3 = []
    subtask_desc_3 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_3,

        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N3):
        thinking3, answer3 = await cot_sc_agents_3[i]([taskInfo, thinking2, answer2], cot_sc_instruction_3, is_sub_task=True)

        possible_answers_3.append(answer3)

    final_decision_agent_3 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking3, answer3 = await final_decision_agent_3([taskInfo, thinking2, answer2] + possible_thinkings_3 + possible_answers_3, "Sub-task 1: Synthesize explicit inradius value.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 4 output: thinking - {thinking3.content}; answer - {answer3.content}")
    subtask_desc_3['response'] = {"thinking": thinking3, "answer": answer3}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_3)
    print("Step 3: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    debate_instr_4 = "Sub-task 1: Decompose the simplified inradius expression into components m, n, p, verify their properties, and compute the sum m + n + p as the final answer. Given solutions to the problem from other agents, consider their opinions as additional advice. Please think carefully and provide an updated answer."
    debate_agents_4 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Debate Agent", model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.5) for role in self.debate_role]
    N4 = self.max_round
    all_thinking4 = [[] for _ in range(N4)]
    all_answer4 = [[] for _ in range(N4)]
    subtask_desc_4 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": debate_instr_4,
        "context": ["user query", thinking3.content, answer3.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Debate"
    }
    for r in range(N4):
        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents_4):
            if r == 0:
                thinking4, answer4 = await agent([taskInfo, thinking3, answer3], debate_instr_4, r, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos_4 = [taskInfo, thinking3, answer3] + all_thinking4[r-1] + all_answer4[r-1]
                thinking4, answer4 = await agent(input_infos_4, debate_instr_4, r, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, analyzing inradius components, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
            all_thinking4[r].append(thinking4)
            all_answer4[r].append(answer4)
    final_decision_agent_4 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking4, answer4 = await final_decision_agent_4([taskInfo, thinking3, answer3] + all_thinking4[-1] + all_answer4[-1], "Sub-task 1: Given all the above thinking and answers, reason over them carefully and provide a final answer.", is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Final Decision agent, calculating final sum m+n+p, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5 output: thinking - {thinking4.content}; answer - {answer4.content}")
    subtask_desc_4['response'] = {"thinking": thinking4, "answer": answer4}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_4)
    print("Step 4: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking4, answer4, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs

async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_sc_N = self.max_sc
    debate_rounds = self.max_round

    # Stage 1: Verify tetrahedron edge length properties and existence of incenter (SC_CoT)
    cot_sc_instruction_1_1 = (
        "Sub-task 1: Symbolically verify the tetrahedron's edge length properties and symmetry constraints, "
        "confirming the existence of the incenter and preparing exact symbolic expressions for subsequent calculations. "
        "Use the given edge lengths and analyze the implications of opposite edges being equal. "
        "Provide symbolic reasoning without numeric approximation."
    )
    cot_sc_agents_1_1 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(cot_sc_N)]
    possible_answers_1_1 = []
    possible_thinkings_1_1 = []
    subtask_desc_1_1 = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_1.subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_1_1,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(cot_sc_N):
        thinking, answer = await cot_sc_agents_1_1[i]([taskInfo], cot_sc_instruction_1_1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_sc_agents_1_1[i].id}, verifying edge properties, thinking: {thinking.content}; answer: {answer.content}")
        possible_answers_1_1.append(answer)
        possible_thinkings_1_1.append(thinking)
    final_decision_agent_1_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking_1_1, answer_1_1 = await final_decision_agent_1_1([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_1_1 + possible_answers_1_1, "Sub-task 1: Synthesize and confirm symbolic verification of tetrahedron edge properties and incenter existence.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Stage 1 Subtask 1 output: thinking - {thinking_1_1.content}; answer - {answer_1_1.content}")
    subtask_desc_1_1['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_1_1, "answer": answer_1_1}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_1_1)
    print("Step 1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_decision_agent_4_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking_4_2, answer_4_2 = await final_decision_agent_4_2([taskInfo, thinking_4_1, answer_4_1] + all_thinking_4_2[-1] + all_answer_4_2[-1], "Sub-task 2: Final verification and sum computation.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Stage 4 Subtask 2 output: thinking - {thinking_4_2.content}; answer - {answer_4_2.content}")
    subtask_desc_4_2['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_4_2, "answer": answer_4_2}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_4_2)
    print("Step 9: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking_4_2, answer_4_2, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs

Given V = 12 and the tetrahedron has four congruent faces with sides √41, √80, and √89, the total surface area S = 4 × area of one face. Using Heron's formula, the area of one face A = √[s(s - √41)(s - √80)(s - √89)] with s = (√41 + √80 + √89)/2.
